As entertaining as this is, it was written by a person that unfortunately lacks the knowledge of astrophysics or orbital mechanics, and the understanding of information technologies.  The elephant in the room is that SCP-2399 is extragalactic in origin and that it is communicating by means of electromagnetic waves (AKA radio) with it's point of origin - this would make extremely difficult if not impossible, due to the fact that radio waves travel at the speed of light. Any intergalactic radio transmission would take billions of years to reach our nearest neighboring galaxy, assuming that it doesn't dissipate, refract under gravitational influence, or become absorbed by various celestial bodies. This means of radio communication would require amounts of energy multiple orders of magnitude greater than it is necessary to destroy a planet, or even a star system for that matter. As SCP-2399 has been produced by an extraterrestrial intelligence, it is a statistical impossibility that they use the same architecture or even principles in computational technology, and factoring in the intergalactic communication capabilities, and immense technological and historical disparity between our civilizations, it would be impossible to comprehend or decipher the communique in question...  And I'm just scratching the surface here - SCP-2399 is made of a material that can withstand the pressure of Jovian lower atmosphere, but becomes damaged by crashing into IO? How exactly was the object observed in the 1st place, since lower atmospheric strata on Jupiter are completely obscured by it's upper atmosphere? What about Jovian gravity? If SCP-2399's drones can just nonchalantly break out of Jupiter's gravity well and just float around looking for parts to facilitate repairs, it would be quite probable that they would be capable of completely replicating SCP-2399 in the first place. How do the human satellites manage to shoot a projectile fast enough to deorbit it from high Jupiter orbit, and so accurately that they almost manage to hit the damn thing? What are the projectiles made of to withstand aerobraking in Jupiter's higher atmosphere? How come recoil from firing doesn't eject the satellite from the Solar system? Just how much energy do these human made satellites even have at their disposal? How'd you manage to send out so many in such a short amount of time, since it takes 7 years to reach Jupiter orbit? And how did you build and launch a rocket 5 times larger than Saturn-5 without anybody noticing and panicking into a nuclear war? And how do you plan to fire an EMP past the Jovian magnetosphere without it dissipating? Also, how do you plan to aerobrake the nukes without them disintegrating from physical stress?  Why don't you just use another one of God tier SCP's to destroy the damn thing? I mean, we got demonic girls, teleportation gates and continent sized invertebrates and whatnot back in the foundation, and you're telling me this thing is indestructible??  And the biggest question of all - if you have the technology to travel faster than light, why not just toss a giant meteor of tungsten at relativistic speeds and make a so-called Relativistic Kill Vehicle, AKA ecocidal weapon of mass destruction? No stress, no fuss, just chuck it really really fast and it'll ruin somebody's day with no discernable warning whatsoever.

So, proposal time.  I notice almost all proposals on this SCP have been to destroy it by any means necessary, along with figuring out how to, but there is one thing I notice no one has really considered, and that is taking it over.  Now hear me out on this one, so far they know how to decode the incoming signals, along with blocking said signals, but, what if the foundation sent their own message, designed to be almost a exact replica of the messages being sent by whoever sent it, with orders to either self destruct, disassemble, or, and this is the best one that could be potentially done, assign allegiance with the people of earth and ignore further orders from home galaxy. This is a very low chance of success, but considering that they have not even bothered considering using other KETER class entities to combat the Destroyer, it is safe to assume that the technology is advanced to such a degree that it surpasses the near magical properties of some of the most terrifying ones out there.

Doctor Rubber is in charge of sharing concise information to the lower members of the foundation, and is also in charge of making introductional videos for D-class and test subjects. Mr. Rubber uses his artistic talent to make short animated videos about different SCP entities, and puts them on display for D-class to understand the SCP thoroughly. His simplification of extremely dangerous SCP's has given him some scorning from the rest of the Foundation Heads, but it has in turn gained him respect from many D-class and other members of the Foundation.

You'd enjoy SCP-4242 ("Foundations"). It's a basement in a church that leads to churches, temples, and shrines of other places around the world in the past, all charged with protecting humanity and the world from anomalies. Some of the people from these historic times were brought into the present day to help with containment or to become agents today. EM communication from the Triangulum Galaxy, especially when in response to anything happening now, is nonsensical as such communications would take over 2.73 million years one way!  So either the communications aren't from/with the Triangulum Galaxy that's ~2.73 million light years away, or their EM based communications also use time travel.  (To those readers that don't know, visible light, xrays, microwaves, ultraviolet, infrared, etc are all just different frequencies of EM radiation) I'm not even going in the idea that the entire thing is a prank on the SCP foundation and humanity, but it's not like I can totally rule that out either...

Now I was thinking and I think I may have come up with a possible solution to the problem centering around destroying SCP-2399. The problem is that they can't destroy it from the outside with any weapons due to its defense systems. But I think that's the problem, the foundation has been trying to destroy it from the outside but what if they destroyed it from the inside.   Now I don't know if this has already been proposed or not but we know that the foundation can intercept and stop messages sent to SCP-2399 through a series of satellites around Jupiter. So what if instead they used the capabilities of these satellites to their advantage by sending their own transmissions and messages to 2399, but inside these messages would be that of none other than a virus.   Think about it, a piece of machinery this advanced has to run on some system to continuously run it and control the drones that exit 2399 as well as detect any projectiles meaning to try and destroy 2399. So what if the foundation could send a message to 2399 that contains a virus that could infiltrate the inside of whatever system is keeping 2399 running. Now you may be thinking that it may have some form of security towards that possibly but that's why I say that the foundation first does everything it can to weaken that security through a series of viruses sent and undeniably intercepted by 2399 like that of a trojan horse that it can't deny, so that way a virus could pass through the security and take down the system with this possibly being how the foundation can take out its defense systems (even if temporarily) and then destroy 2399.  So tell me what do you all think of my proposal

Here's an idea: Talk to the aliens. Just talk to them. It's that simple. If you launch bigger bombs, it'll just make the aliens more angry. I can think of two reasons the aliens would want to attack us. Either the aliens don't know much about us, and are worried we'll try to destroy them, or they think we're not advanced enough to be worth anything, and we might as well all die. TALKING TO THEM WILL SOLVE BOTH OF THESE PROBLEMS. And if they still want to kill us, go ahead and use the bombs. Throwing bombs at them without communicating with them is like throwing toothbrushes to kill a dragon. It's never gonna work, and it's just gonna cost a lot. And then when you realize small toothbrushes don't work, YOU JUST THROW BIGGER ONES. BY THE TIME YOU CAN GET A TOOTHBRUSH BIG ENOUGH TO KILL THE DRAGON, IT'S ALREADY HAD TIME TO BURN DOWN THE VILLAGE. AND ESCAPE. NOW YOU'RE DEAD. If you lure the dragon out if the village then no one has to die. And if that doesn't work, THEN you start throwing toothbrushes. Bombs should be used if all else fails, not as a first attempt. I can't believe nobody has thought of this. And sure, the technology needed to contact the aliens is expensive, but so are the bombs, and if spending a few extra pennies on advanced technology could prevent the apocalypse, It's probably worth it.

[12]Rejoice, and be exceeding glad: for great is your reward in heaven: for so persecuted they the prophets which were before you. [13]Ye are the salt of the earth: but if the salt have lost his savour, wherewith shall it be salted? it is thenceforth good for nothing, but to be cast out, and to be trodden under foot of men. [14]Ye are the light of the world. A city that is set on an hill cannot be hid. [15]Neither do men light a candle, and put it under a bushel, but on a candlestick; and it giveth light unto all that are in the house. [16]Let your light so shine before men, that they may see your good works, and glorify your Father which is in heaven. [17]Think not that I am come to destroy the law, or the prophets: I am not come to destroy, but to fulfil. [18]For verily I say unto you, Till heaven and earth pass, one jot or one tittle shall in no wise pass from the law, till all be fulfilled. [19]Whosoever therefore shall break one of these least commandments, and shall teach men so, he shall be called the least in the kingdom of heaven: but whosoever shall do and teach them, the same shall be called great in the kingdom of heaven. [20]For I say unto you, That except your righteousness shall exceed the righteousness of the scribes and Pharisees, ye shall in no case enter into the kingdom of heaven. [21]Ye have heard that it was said by them of old time, Thou shalt not kill; and whosoever shall kill shall be in danger of the judgment: [22]But I say unto you, That whosoever is angry with his brother without a cause shall be in danger of the judgment: and whosoever shall say to his brother, Raca, shall be in danger of the council: but whosoever shall say, Thou fool, shall be in danger of hell fire. [23]Therefore if thou bring thy gift to the altar, and there rememberest that thy brother hath ought against thee; [24]Leave there thy gift before the altar, and go thy way; first be reconciled to thy brother, and then come and offer thy gift. [25]Agree with thine adversary quickly, whiles thou art in the way with him; lest at any time the adversary deliver thee to the judge, and the judge deliver thee to the officer, and thou be cast into prison. [26]Verily I say unto thee, Thou shalt by no means come out thence, till thou hast paid the uttermost farthing. [27]Ye have heard that it was said by them of old time, Thou shalt not commit adultery: [28]But I say unto you, That whosoever looketh on a woman to lust after her hath committed adultery with her already in his heart. [29]And if thy right eye offend thee, pluck it out, and cast it from thee: for it is profitable for thee that one of thy members should perish, and not that thy whole body should be cast into hell. [30]And if thy right hand offend thee, cut it off, and cast it from thee: for it is profitable for thee that one of thy members should perish, and not that thy whole body should be cast into hell. [31]It hath been said, Whosoever shall put away his wife, let him give her a writing of divorcement: [32]But I say unto you, That whosoever shall put away his wife, saving for the cause of fornication, causeth her to commit adultery: and whosoever shall marry her that is divorced committeth adultery. [33]Again, ye have heard that it hath been said by them of old time, Thou shalt not forswear thyself, but shalt perform unto the Lord thine oaths: [34]But I say unto you, Swear not at all; neither by heaven; for it is God's throne: [35]Nor by the earth; for it is his footstool: neither by Jerusalem; for it is the city of the great King. [36]Neither shalt thou swear by thy head, because thou canst not make one hair white or black. [37]But let your communication be, Yea, yea; Nay, nay: for whatsoever is more than these cometh of evil. [38]Ye have heard that it hath been said, An eye for an eye, and a tooth for a tooth: [39]But I say unto you, That ye resist not evil: but whosoever shall smite thee on thy right cheek, turn to him the other also. [40]And if any man will sue thee at the law, and take away thy coat, let him have thy cloke also. [41]And whosoever shall compel thee to go a mile, go with him twain. [42]Give to him that asketh thee, and from him that would borrow of thee turn not thou away. [43]Ye have heard that it hath been said, Thou shalt love thy neighbour, and hate thine enemy. [44]But I say unto you, Love your enemies, bless them that curse you, do good to them that hate you, and pray for them which despitefully use you, and persecute you; [45]That ye may be the children of your Father which is in heaven: for he maketh his sun to rise on the evil and on the good, and sendeth rain on the just and on the unjust. [46]For if ye love them which love you, what reward have ye? do not even the publicans the same? [47]And if ye salute your brethren only, what do ye more than others? do not even the publicans so? 8
Ah, yes, 2399 fell victim to the same unstoppable super-weapon as the dinosaurs, a big rock.  Seriously, for all the horrifying things in the SCP universe, it's worth remembering that all it took to wipe out life that had been dominant on Earth for *billions* of years was a fucking *rock* less than a *thousandth* its size. And it's only by sheer luck that humanity hasn't been wiped out in a similar manner.
